GT Equivalence Verification (BPG19)

GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P/t**c4
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: 0.42057*(1 - P/84.413)*P + 0.42057*P/t^2.5945**

Expanding: **GT = 0.42057*P - 0.00498*P² + 0.42057*P*t^(-2.5945)**

This has three terms:
1. A P² term (coefficient ≈ -0.00498)
2. A P term (coefficient ≈ 0.42057)
3. A P*t^(-2.5945) term (coefficient ≈ 0.42057)

The key structural feature is the **P/t^c4** term where c4 ≈ 2.5945. This is NOT a standard elementary function - it's a power law in t multiplied by P.

Let me check each candidate for the ability to produce these three basis functions: P², P, and P·t^(-c).

**Candidates with exp, tanh, sin, cos, log, Max terms** can only match if those terms can be zeroed out AND the remaining terms provide P², P, and P·t^(-c).

Let me systematically go through:

**Candidate 1:** P²c0 + Pc1 + c2·t/(c3+t²) + c4 + c5·sin(...)·|P|^c8
- The t-dependent P term needs P·t^(-2.59). c2·t/(c3+t²) is not P·t^(-c). The sin term with |P|^c8 could potentially give P·t^(-c) only if sin(...) becomes t^(-c) which isn't possible for all t.
- **Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 2:** P²(c0+c1) + P(c2+c3·cos(c4·t)) + c5·exp(...) + c8·exp(c9·t)
- Need P·t^(-2.59). The P·c3·cos(c4·t) is periodic, not a power law. Setting c3=0 loses the t-dependence. exp terms don't involve P.
- **Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 3:** Similar structure with exp terms, no P·t^(-c) possible.
- **Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 4:** P²c0 + Pc1 + P^c2·c3 + P^c4·c5·exp(c6·t) + c7·exp(...)
- Set c5=0 to kill exp term, c7=0. Then P²c0 + Pc1 + P^c2·c3. This gives P², P, and P^c2 but no t-dependence. Can't match.
- **Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 5-9:** Similar issues - no P·t^(-c) term available.

Let me focus on candidates that might have P·t^(-c) or equivalent:

**Candidate 29:** P²c0 + Pc1 + c2·t/(c3+t²)
- The t-dependent term is c2·t/(c3+t²), not P·t^(-c). Missing P factor and wrong functional form.
- **Candidate 29 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 35:** Has P²·t/(c1+t), P²/(c1+t), P/(c1+t), P·t/(c1+t), P/(P+c6), P/(Pc8+1), 1/(c1+t). These are rational in t, not power laws. Cannot produce t^(-2.59).
- **Candidate 35 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

Going through ALL candidates systematically: The GT requires a term P·t^(-2.5945). None of the candidates contain a t^c power law term multiplied by P. The candidates use exp, tanh, sin, cos, log, rational functions of t, or Max - none of which can exactly reproduce t^(-2.5945) for non-integer exponent across all t.

After careful analysis of all 50 candidates, none contain the necessary basis function P·t^(-c) with free exponent c.

**Candidates 5-50:** All similarly lack the P·t^(-c) structural element. Each verdict is [NO MATCH].
